          <h4>
           Email
          </h4>
          <h3>
           Share team inboxes
          </h3>
          <p>
           Whether you have a team of 2 or 200, Mailboxes keep everyone on the same page.
Leverage automation to move fast, while always giving customers a human, helpful experience.
          </p>
